| FSM/Emp/03                                                             | Employee flow                                                |                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Validate if the "Waiting for disposal" application status is added in the filter \_English.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Functional                                         | <p></p><p></p><ol><li>Login as a ULB Employee on the mSeva portal with English language.</li><li>Navigate to FSM.</li><li>Go to the employee inbox.</li><li>Validate that the "Waiting for disposal" application status is added in the filter.</li><li>Validate "Waiting for disposal" under the “Application Status” and show “-” under “SLA Days Remaining.”</li><li>The status should also reflect on the application timeline when a user clicks on the application.</li></ol>                                                                                                             | <ol><li>User should be able to filter out the application on the basis of the "Waiting for disposal" filter.</li><li>User is able to see the "Waiting for disposal" under “Application Status” and “-” under “SLA Days Remaining.”</li><li>The status should also reflect on the application timeline when a user clicks on the application.</li></ol>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | <ol><li>User should be able to filter out the application on basis of the "Waiting for disposal" filter.</li><li>User is able to see "Waiting for disposal" under “Application Status” and “-” under “SLA Days Remaining.”</li><li>Status should also reflect on the application timeline when a user clicks on the application.</li></ol>                                                                                                     | Done       | Done       |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | <ol><li>User should be able to filter out the application on the basis of the "Waiting for disposal" filter.</li><li>User is able to see "Waiting for disposal" under the “Application Status” and “-” under “SLA Days Remaining.”</li><li>The status should also reflect on the application timeline when a user clicks on the application.</li></ol>                                                                                         | PASSED     |            | UAT
